## TOPIC 02089: PropertyObject.IsAliasObject

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-isaliasobject.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-isaliasobject.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.IsAliasObject( lookupString, options) Return Value Boolean Returns True if the property is an alias. Purpose Returns a value that indicates whether the subproperty the lookupString parameter specifies is an alias to another object. Remarks An alias object is a property object t

### PropertyObject.IsAliasObject

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).IsAliasObject( lookupString, options)

#### Return Value

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

Returns
 True
 if the property is an alias.

#### Purpose

Returns a value that indicates whether the subproperty the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies is an alias to another object.

#### Remarks

An alias object is a property object that references another object or array element.

Create an alias object by using the
 [PropOption_NotOwning](propertyoptions.html)
 option with the
 [PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject](propertyobject-setpropertyobject.html)
 or
 [PropertyObject.SetPropertyObjectByOffset](propertyobject-setpropertyobjectbyoffset.html)
 methods.

You can also create an alias object by calling the
 [PropertyObject.GetPropertyObject](propertyobject-getpropertyobject.html)
 or
 [PropertyObject.GetPropertyObjectByOffset](propertyobject-getpropertyobjectbyoffset.html)
 methods on arrays that do not contain objects (such as arrays of numbers, Booleans, strings or ActiveX references), in which case the resulting alias object refers to the specified array element. With the exception of the
 [PropertyObject.Parent](propertyobject-parent.html)
 property, calling a method or referencing a property on an alias object is equivalent to calling the same method or property on the referenced object or array element unless you pass the
 [PropOption_ReferToAlias](propertyoptions.html)
 option, in which case the method affects the alias object itself. To obtain the referenced object, use the GetPropertyObject method and pass an empty string for the
 lookupString
 parameter.

TestStand uses alias objects to make objects appear to have multiple owners. For example, the
 [SequenceContext](sequencecontext.html)
 object contains an alias to the current step. The
 [Step](step.html)
 object cannot be a subproperty of the sequence context because it belongs to the sequence instead. By having an alias object that refers to the step, the sequence context appears to contain the step itself.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

#### See Also

[Lookup Strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)

[PropertyObject.GetPropertyObject](propertyobject-getpropertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject.GetPropertyObjectByOffset](propertyobject-getpropertyobjectbyoffset.html)

[PropertyObject.Parent](propertyobject-parent.html)

[PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject](propertyobject-setpropertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject.SetPropertyObjectByOffset](propertyobject-setpropertyobjectbyoffset.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Methods

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobject-isequalto.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02090: PropertyObject.IsEqualTo

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-isequalto.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-isequalto.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.IsEqualTo( objectToCompare, options) Return Value Boolean Purpose Compares this object to another PropertyObject. Remarks With no options, this method returns True if both objects have the same number of subproperties with the same case-insensitive names, value types, represent

### PropertyObject.IsEqualTo

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).IsEqualTo( objectToCompare, options)

#### Return Value

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Compares this object to another PropertyObject.

#### Remarks

With no options, this method returns
 True
 if both objects have the same number of subproperties with the same case-insensitive names, value types, representation, values, flags, and attributes. If both objects are type definitions, the struct/cluster passing settings, type flags, instance default flags, instance override flags, type versions, type definition lock settings, and type attributes must also be the same.

If a subproperty enables the
 [PropFlags_ExcludeFromComparison](propertyflags.html)
 flag, TestStand ignores the subproperty for purposes of this comparison.

If you specify the
 [PropOption_RequireIdenticalStructure](propertyoptions.html)
 option, additional settings for the properties must be the same. If you specify the
 PropOption_CaseInsensitive
 option, the method ignores case differences when comparing string values.

#### Parameters

objectToCompare
 As
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[In] Specifies the object to compare to this object.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

You typically use the
 [PropOption_CaseInsensitive](propertyoptions.html)
 ,
 [PropOption_DoNotRecurse](propertyoptions.html)
 , and
 [PropOption_RequireIdenticalStructure](propertyoptions.html)
 options with this method.

#### See Also

[PropertyFlags](propertyflags.html)

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Methods

### PropertyObject.IsModifiedType

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).IsModifiedType

#### Data Type

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Returns or specifies the
 [PropTypeFlags_IsModifiedType](propertyobjtypeflags.html)
 flag on the current
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)
 .

#### Remarks

Calling the
 [PropertyObject.SetTypeFlags](propertyobject-settypeflags.html)

 [PropertyObjTypeFlags](propertyobjtypeflags.html)

 PropTypeFlags_IsModifiedType
 flag, so you cannot clear the
 PropTypeFlags_IsModifiedType
 flag with the
 SetTypeFlags
 method. Use this property instead to clear the

 flag.

This property is valid only for PropertyObject objects that are type definitions. Use the

 property to determine whether a PropertyObject is a type definition.

### PropertyObject.IsRootTypeDefinition

## TOPIC 02095: PropertyObject.Name

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-name.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-name.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.Name Data Type String Purpose Specifies the name of the PropertyObject. Remarks TestStand expressions require PropertyObject names to be strings that contain only letters, numbers, and underscores. PropertyObject names cannot contain spaces, start with a number, or be empty. Ad

### PropertyObject.Name

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).Name

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies the name of the PropertyObject.

#### Remarks

TestStand expressions require PropertyObject names to be strings that contain only letters, numbers, and underscores. PropertyObject names cannot contain spaces, start with a number, or be empty. Additionally, the PropertyObject name cannot be "
 Value
 ", and you cannot have duplicate subproperty names. For example,
 MyVariableName_2000
 is a valid PropertyObject name. Names of elements in a PropertyObject array can contain any character. Both sequence names and step names are examples of such named array elements. However, sequence names cannot be empty or contain control characters. You cannot have duplicate sequence names. The name
 NI
 is reserved at the root level for attribute names.

Note

Note

PropertyObject.ValidateNewName

PropertyObject.ValidateNewSubPropertyName

PropertyObject.ValidateNewElementName

TypeUsageList.ValidateNewTypeName

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.GetDisplayNames](propertyobject-getdisplaynames.html)

[PropertyObject.ValidateNewElementName](propertyobject-validatenewelementname.html)

[PropertyObject.ValidateNewName](propertyobject-validatenewname.html)

[PropertyObject.ValidateNewSubPropertyName](propertyobject-validatenewsubpropertyname.html)

[Sequence.Name](sequence-name.html)

[Step.Name](step-name.html)

[StepType.Name](steptype-name.html)

[TypeUsageList.ValidateNewTypeName](typeusagelist-validatenewtypename.html)

## TOPIC 02097: PropertyObject.NumericFormat

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-numericformat.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-numericformat.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.NumericFormat Data Type String Purpose Specifies a numeric format string TestStand uses to format a numeric value or values in a numeric array when you call the PropertyObject.GetFormattedValue method. Remarks The syntax of the numeric format string is identical to the format s

### PropertyObject.NumericFormat

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).NumericFormat

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies a numeric format string TestStand uses to format a numeric value or values in a numeric array when you call the
 [PropertyObject.GetFormattedValue](propertyobject-getformattedvalue.html)
 method.

#### Remarks

The syntax of the numeric format string is identical to the format string that the C
 printf
 function accepts, with the following exceptions:

- Place a
 $ 
 character after the
 % 
 character in the format string to remove trailing zeros after the decimal point.
- Use a format code of
 %b 
 to format a number in binary.
- Specify an empty string to set the format to the default numeric format.

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.GetDisplayNames](propertyobject-getdisplaynames.html)

[PropertyObject.GetFormattedValue](propertyobject-getformattedvalue.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Properties

## TOPIC 02101: PropertyObject.Search

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-search.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-search.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.Search( lookupString, searchString, searchOptions, filterOptions, elementsToSearch, limitToAdapters, limitToNamedProps, limitToPropsOfNamedTypes, subpropLookupStringsToExclude) Return Value SearchResults A SearchResult object. Purpose Searches a property object and subpropertie

### PropertyObject.Search

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).Search( lookupString, searchString, searchOptions, filterOptions, elementsToSearch, limitToAdapters, limitToNamedProps, limitToPropsOfNamedTypes, subpropLookupStringsToExclude)

#### Return Value

[SearchResults](searchresults.html)

A SearchResult object.

#### Purpose

Searches a property object and subproperties.

#### Remarks

Returns a
 [SearchResults](searchresults.html)
 object that is a handle to the asynchronous search already in progress. To wait for the search to complete, call the
 [SearchResults.IsComplete](searchresults-iscomplete.html)
 method.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies a lookup string that indicates the location of the subproperty of the PropertyObject on which to begin the search. If a match is found, the location of the match in the
 [SearchMatch](searchmatch.html)
 object is relative to the original PropertyObject, not the subproperty. You can pass an empty string for this parameter to begin the search at the root-level of the PropertyObject.

searchString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the string or regular expression for which to search. To use regular expressions, you must pass the option
 SearchOptions_RegExpr
 for the
 searchOptions
 parameter of this method.

searchOptions
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies one or more
 [SearchOptions](searchoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple search options. The search option
 SearchOptions_IncludeSubsequenceFiles
 does not apply to this method.

filterOptions
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies one or more
 [SearchFilterOptions](searchfilteroptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple search filter options. Only the following filter options apply to this method:
 SearchFilterOptions_CustomStepProps
 ,
 SearchFilterOptions_BuiltinStepProps
 , and
 SearchFilterOptions_ModuleStepProps
 .

elementsToSearch
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies one or more
 [SearchElements](searchelements.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple elements to search.

limitToAdapters
 As
 [String Array](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array of
 [AdapterKeyNames](adapterkeynames.html)
 constants to indicate the steps of which adapters to search. Pass an empty array or
 NULL
 to search steps that use any adapter.

limitToNamedProps
 As
 [String Array](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array of property names under which to limit the search. Pass an empty array or
 NULL
 to search all properties. If you specify names of properties to which to limit the search, TestStand searches only those properties with the names you specify and all their subproperties.

limitToPropsOfNamedTypes
 As
 [String Array](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array of type names to which to limit the search. Pass an empty array or
 NULL
 to search instances of all types. Use this parameter to limit the search instances of all types. Use this parameter to limit the search to instances of the types you specify.

subpropLookupStringsToExclude
 As
 [String Array](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array of lookup strings that indicate which subproperties to exclude from the search. Pass an empty array or
 NULL
 if you do not want to exclude any properties. You can pass a lookup string with the wildcard character (
 *
 ) in place of any property name to indicate that all properties match that part of the lookup string. You can also use the wildcard character to match any element of an array by specifying the wildcard character (
 *
 ) for the array element index. For example, if the property object you search is an array of steps, you can specify the lookup string
 "[*].Result"
 to exclude the
 Result
 property of all steps in the array.

Note

#### See Also

[AdapterKeyNames](adapterkeynames.html)

[Engine.SearchFiles](engine-searchfiles.html)

[SearchElements](searchelements.html)

[SearchFilterOptions](searchfilteroptions.html)

[SearchMatch](searchmatch.html)

[SearchOptions](searchoptions.html)

[SearchResults](searchresults.html)

[SearchResults.IsComplete](searchresults-iscomplete.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Remarks If you call this method on an alias object , TestStand generates the stream using the object to which the alias refers. This method does not include alias subpr

### PropertyObject.Serialize

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).Serialize( stream, objectName, RWoptions)

#### Purpose

Adds the contents of the object to a stream of string data.

#### Remarks

If you call this method on an
 [alias object](propertyobject-isaliasobject.html)
 , TestStand generates the stream using the object to which the alias refers. This method does not include alias subproperty objects in the stream.

#### Parameters

stream
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In/Out] Specifies an existing string or an empty string. The method returns a new string that contains the contents of the string passed for this parameter and the contents of the object.

objectName
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the name with which to store the object in the stream.

RWoptions
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [ReadWriteOptions](readwriteoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple read/write options.

## TOPIC 02103: PropertyObject.SetDimensions

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setdimensions.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setdimensions.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetDimensions( lookupString, options, lowerBounds, upperBounds) Purpose This method is obsolete. Use the PropertyObjectType.ArrayDimensions property instead. Remarks Sets the upper and lower bounds for the array the lookupString parameter specifies. Use the PropertyObject.SetNu

### PropertyObject.SetDimensions

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetDimensions( lookupString, options, lowerBounds, upperBounds)

#### Purpose

Note

PropertyObjectType.ArrayDimensions

#### Remarks

Sets the upper and lower bounds for the array the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies.

Use the
 [PropertyObject.SetNumElements](propertyobject-setnumelements.html)
 method to set the size of a one-dimensional array.

To insert a new array element in a one-dimensional array at the specified offset, use the
 Set_ByOffset
 methods of the PropertyObject class and specify the
 PropOption_InsertElement
 flag.

To delete specific elements from a one-dimensional array, use the
 [PropertyObject.DeleteElements](propertyobject-deleteelements.html)
 method.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

lowerBounds
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array index string describing the lowest valid index for each dimension. For example, a two-dimensional array with a lower bound of 0 for the first dimension and 2 for the second has the lower bound string "[0][2]".

upperBounds
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an array index string describing the highest valid index for each dimension. For example, a two-dimensional array with an upper bound of 2 for the first dimension and 4 for the second would have the upper bound string "[2][4]".

#### See Also

[Lookup Strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)

[PropertyObject.DeleteElements](propertyobject-deleteelements.html)

### PropertyObject.SetInstanceDefaultFlags

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetInstanceDefaultFlags( lookupString, options, Flags)

#### Purpose

Sets the default flags for instances of the type the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies.

#### Remarks

This method is valid only for type definitions. The type instance default flags are the initial flags instances of the type have when they are created. If the corresponding instance override flag is set, the value for that flag as defined in the instance default flag will always be the value in the instance of the type and cannot be changed in that instance.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

Flags
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the default
 [flags](propertyflags.html)
 of the type.

## TOPIC 02109: PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setpropertyobject.html`

- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject( lookupString, options, newValue) Purpose Sets the subproperty the lookupString parameter specifies to the PropertyObject object you pass. Remarks Do not call this method if another object already contains the object the newValue parameter specifies. For examp

### PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetPropertyObject( lookupString, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the subproperty the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies to the PropertyObject object you pass.

#### Remarks

Do not call this method if another object already contains the object the
 newValue
 parameter specifies. For example, if the object you want to specify for the
 newValue
 parameter is already a subproperty or an array element of another object, it cannot also be the subproperty of a different object. You can work around this issue by using the
 [PropOption_NotOwning](propertyoptions.html)
 option when you call this method to instead create an alias to the object, by using the
 [PropertyObject.Clone](propertyobject-clone.html)
 method to make a copy of the object and use the copy instead, or by removing the object from its current parent or array before assigning a new parent.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the property.

#### See Also

[Engine.NewPropertyObject](engine-newpropertyobject.html)

[Lookup Strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject.Clone](propertyobject-clone.html)

[PropertyObject.GetPropertyObject](propertyobject-getpropertyobject.html)

## TOPIC 02110: PropertyObject.SetPropertyObjectByOffset

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setpropertyobjectbyoffset.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setpropertyobjectbyoffset.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetPropertyObjectByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue) Purpose Sets the array element the arrayOffset parameter specifies to the PropertyObject object you pass. Remarks This method is valid only for array objects. For arrays that do not contain objects, such as arrays of nu

### PropertyObject.SetPropertyObjectByOffset

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetPropertyObjectByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the array element the
 arrayOffset
 parameter specifies to the PropertyObject object you pass.

#### Remarks

This method is valid only for array objects. For arrays that do not contain objects, such as arrays of numbers, Booleans, strings, or ActiveX references, this method expects a property object of the same type as the array element.

Do not call this method if another object already contains the object the
 newValue
 parameter specifies. For example, if the object you want to specify for the
 newValue
 parameter is already a subproperty or an array element of another object, it cannot also be the subproperty of a different object. You can work around this issue by using the
 [PropOption_NotOwning](propertyoptions.html)
 option when you call this method to instead create an alias to the object, by using the
 [PropertyObject.Clone](propertyobject-clone.html)
 method to make a copy of the object and use the copy instead, or by removing the object from its current parent or array before assigning a new parent.

#### Parameters

arrayOffset
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies a zero-based number representing the offset of an array element in the one-dimensional physical storage of the array. The offset is in terms of the number of elements.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the array element.

#### See Also

[Engine.NewPropertyObject](engine-newpropertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject.Clone](propertyobject-clone.html)

[PropertyObject.GetPropertyObjectByOffset](propertyobject-getpropertyobjectbyoffset.html)

[PropertyObject.SetPropertyObject](propertyobject-setpropertyobject.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setsubpropertyindex.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setsubpropertyindex.html

- page_type: `leaf`

PropertyObject

#### Parameters

newValue
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies one of the supported

 .

 [Variant](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] [
 [Optional](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_optional_parameters)
 ] Specifies the password you require to unlock the type. This password can be empty only if the value for the
 newValue
 parameter is
 ProtectedObjectOption_None
 . TestStand uses this password and the password history of a type during

 to determine whether a newer version of the type can replace an older version without requiring the password for the older version.

## TOPIC 02114: PropertyObject.SetValBinary

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalbinary.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalbinary.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetValBinary( lookupString, options, newValue) Purpose Sets the string value of the property the lookupString parameter specifies to contain a string representation of the binary data you pass to the newValue parameter. This method compresses the binary data and then encodes th

### PropertyObject.SetValBinary

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValBinary( lookupString, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the string value of the property the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies to contain a string representation of the binary data you pass to the
 newValue
 parameter. This method compresses the binary data and then encodes the compressed data into the string using only printable ASCII characters.

#### Remarks

Ordinarily, you cannot store binary data in a string because strings cannot contain zero bytes and strings must not contain invalid multibyte character set (MBCS) sequences. However, by encoding binary data using only printable non-MBCS-lead-byte characters, this method enables you to store arbitrary binary data in TestStand string variables or properties.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [Byte Array](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the array of bytes to store in the string property.

#### See Also

[Lookup Strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)

[PropertyObject.GetValBinary](propertyobject-getvalbinary.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Methods

### PropertyObject.SetValIDispatch

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValIDispatch( lookupString, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the value of the ActiveX Automation Reference property the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies. You must specify the value as an IDispatch pointer.

#### Remarks

The reference property maintains a reference to the object you specify. If the property already contains a reference, it releases that reference before storing the new one. If you specify a
 NULL
 reference, the property releases any existing reference it holds.

Note

PropertyObject.SetValInterface

PropValType_Reference

PropertyObject.SetValInterface

 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [Object](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the property.

     CA_DiscardObjHandle(objHandle);

### PropertyObject.SetValIDispatchByOffset

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValIDispatchByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the value of the ActiveX Automation Reference array element the
 arrayOffset
 parameter specifies.

#### Remarks

This method is valid only for array objects. You must specify the value as an IDispatch pointer.

The reference property maintains a reference to the object you specify. If the property already contains a reference, it releases that reference before storing the new one. If you specify a
 NULL
 reference, the property releases any existing reference it holds.

This method and the
 [PropertyObject.SetValInterfaceByOffset](propertyobject-setvalinterfacebyoffset.html)
 apply to the
 [PropValType_Reference](propertyvaluetypes.html)
 value type. The
 PropertyObject.GetValInterface
 and
 PropertyObject.SetValInterface
 methods are intended for use by advanced users who want to store arbitrary interfaces in TestStand reference properties.

#### Parameters

arrayOffset
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies a zero-based number representing the offset of an array element in the one-dimensional physical storage of the array. The offset is in terms of the number of elements.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [Object](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the array element.

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [IUnknown](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the property.

#### Example

LabWindows/CVI:
     TS_PropertySetValInterface(propObj, &errorInfo,
                                "Locals.ActiveXAutoObj", 0, someObj);

Visual Basic (function call):
     propObj.SetValInterface("Locals.ActiveXAutoObj", 0, someObj)

Visual Basic (inline):
     propObj.Locals.ActiveXAutoObj = someObj

Visual C++:

     propObj->SetValInterface("Locals.ActiveXAutoObj", 0, someObj);

## TOPIC 02122: PropertyObject.SetValInterfaceByOffset

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalinterfacebyoffset.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalinterfacebyoffset.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetValInterfaceByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue) Purpose Sets the value of the ActiveX Automation Reference array element the arrayOffset parameter specifies. Remarks This method is valid only for array objects. You must specify the value as an IUnknown pointer. The ref

### PropertyObject.SetValInterfaceByOffset

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValInterfaceByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the value of the ActiveX Automation Reference array element the
 arrayOffset
 parameter specifies.

#### Remarks

This method is valid only for array objects. You must specify the value as an IUnknown pointer.

The reference property maintains a reference to the object you specify. If the property already contains a reference, it releases that reference before storing the new one. If you specify a
 NULL
 reference, the property releases any existing reference it holds.

This method and the
 [PropertyObject.SetValIDispatchByOffset](propertyobject-setvalidispatchbyoffset.html)
 method apply to the
 [PropValType_Reference](propertyvaluetypes.html)
 value type. The
 PropertyObject.GetValInterface
 and
 PropertyObject.SetValInterface
 methods are intended for use by advanced users who want to store arbitrary interfaces in TestStand reference properties.

#### Parameters

arrayOffset
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies a zero-based number representing the offset of an array element in the one-dimensional physical storage of the array. The offset is in terms of the number of elements.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [IUnknown](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the array element.

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.GetValInterfaceByOffset](propertyobject-getvalinterfacebyoffset.html)

[PropertyObject.SetValIDispatchByOffset](propertyobject-setvalidispatchbyoffset.html)

[PropertyObject.SetValInterface](propertyobject-setvalinterface.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[PropertyValueTypes](propertyvaluetypes.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

### PropertyObject.SetValNumberByOffset

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValNumberByOffset( arrayOffset, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the double-precision, 64-bit floating-point value of the array element the
 arrayOffset
 parameter specifies.

#### Remarks

This method is valid only for array objects and is intended for use with arrays of double-precision, floating-point numbers. Use the
 [PropertyObject.SetValInteger64ByOffset](propertyobject-setvalinteger64byoffset.html)
 method with arrays of 64-bit integers, and use the
 [PropertyObject.SetValUnsignedInteger64ByOffset](propertyobject-setvalunsignedinteger64byoffse.html)
 method with arrays of unsigned 64-bit integers. If the array is of a type other than double-precision, floating-point, you can use this method with the corresponding
 [PropOption_Coerce](propertyoptions.html)
 constant.

#### Parameters

arrayOffset
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies a zero-based number representing the offset of an array element in the one-dimensional physical storage of the array. The offset is in terms of the number of elements.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [Double](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the array element.

## TOPIC 02129: PropertyObject.SetValVariant

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalvariant.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setvalvariant.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetValVariant( lookupString, options, newValue) Purpose Sets the value of the property the lookupString parameter specifies with a variant. Remarks You can use this method to set the value of an entire array at once. When you set an array property using this method, TestStand r

### PropertyObject.SetValVariant

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetValVariant( lookupString, options, newValue)

#### Purpose

Sets the value of the property the
 lookupString
 parameter specifies with a variant.

#### Remarks

You can use this method to set the value of an entire array at once. When you set an array property using this method, TestStand resizes and redefines the dimensions of the destination array to match the array you pass in. Refer to the example in this topic for more information about how to use this method.

#### Parameters

lookupString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass an empty string to denote the PropertyObject to which the method applies, or pass the name of a subproperty within the PropertyObject. You can also pass
 [lookup strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)
 to this parameter.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple options.

newValue
 As
 [Variant](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the new value for the property.

#### Example

LabWindows/CVI:
     VARIANT tmpVariant;
     double numArray[] = {0.123, 1.234, 12.34};

     CA_VariantSet1DArray (&tmpVariant, CAVT_DOUBLE, 3, numArray);
     TS_PropertySetValVariant(propObj, &errorInfo,
                              "Locals.NumArray", 0, tmpVariant);
     CA_VariantClear(tmpVariant);

Visual Basic (function call):
     Dim numArray(2) As Double

     numArray(0) = 0.123
     numArray(1) = 1.234
     numArray(2) = 12.34
     propObj.SetValVariant("Locals.NumArray", 0, numArray)

Visual Basic (inline):
     Dim numArray(2) As Double

     numArray(0) = 0.123
     numArray(1) = 1.234
     numArray(2) = 12.34
     propObj.Locals.NumArray = numArray

Visual C++:
     #include "tsvcutil.h"
     std::vector<double> doubleVector;

     TSUTIL::SafeArray<double, VT_R8> safeArray;
     safeArray.SetFromVector(doubleVector);

     propObj->SetValVariant("Locals.NumArray", 0, safeArray.GetVariant());

#### See Also

[Lookup Strings](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_api_lookupstring)

[PropertyObject.GetValVariant](propertyobject-getvalvariant.html)

[PropertyObject.SetValInteger64](propertyobject-setvalinteger64.html)

[PropertyObject.SetValUnsignedInteger64](propertyobject-setvalunsignedinteger64.html)

[PropertyObject.SetValVariantByOffset](propertyobject-setvalvariantbyoffset.html)

[PropertyOptions](propertyoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Methods

## TOPIC 02131: PropertyObject.SetXML

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-setxml.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-setxml.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.SetXML( xmlStream, reserved1, reserved2 = ConflictHandler_Error) Purpose Reads the contents of a stream of XML string data and stores the contents in the PropertyObject to which the method applies. Remarks You can use the PropertyObject.GetXML method to generate the correspondi

### PropertyObject.SetXML

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).SetXML( xmlStream, reserved1, reserved2 = ConflictHandler_Error)

#### Purpose

Reads the contents of a stream of XML string data and stores the contents in the PropertyObject to which the method applies.

#### Remarks

You can use the
 [PropertyObject.GetXML](propertyobject-getxml.html)
 method to generate the corresponding XML this method requires.

You cannot unserialize a stream that contains a container type into a property object that is a value type, or vice versa. This method does not return an error. Instead, it sets the PropertyObject on which this method operates to the default value.

If you attempt to unserialize a stream that contains a value type into a property object of a different value type, TestStand attempts to coerce the value. If the coercion is unsuccessful, TestStand only resets the PropertyObject on which this method operates to the default value.

TestStand does not assign the name and some flags associated with the top-level PropertyObject in the stream to the PropertyObject on which this method operates.

Refer to the World Wide Web Consortium-compliant XML schema file,
 PropertyObject.xsd
 , located in the
 [<TestStand>](/csh?context=ts_tsfundamentals_directories)
 \Components\Models\TestStandModels
 directory, for more information about the output of the
 PropertyObject.GetXML
 method and the required format for the input stream to this method.

The
 [<TestStand>](/csh?context=ts_tsfundamentals_directories)
 \Components\Models\TestStandModels\Report.xsd
 file defines the XSD schema definition for XML reports.

#### Parameters

xmlStream
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an XML stream.

reserved1
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 .

reserved2
 As
 [TypeConflictHandlerTypes](typeconflicthandlertypes.html)

[In] This parameter is reserved for when the
 [PropertyObject.GetXML](propertyobject-getxml.html)
 method supports storing type information in an XML stream. This parameter specifies how to handle type conflicts in the stream.

This parameter has a default value of
 ConflictHandler_Error
 .

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.GetXML](propertyobject-getxml.html)

[PropertyObject.Serialize](propertyobject-serialize.html)

[PropertyObject.UnserializeEx](propertyobject-unserializeex.html)

[TypeConflictHandlerTypes](typeconflicthandlertypes.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Methods

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.TypeAttributes Data Type PropertyObject Purpose This property is a container for storing data associated with the type definition. Remarks Use container subproperties under the TypeAttributes property to serve as attribute namespaces. National Instruments recommends that you cr

### PropertyObject.TypeAttributes

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).TypeAttributes

#### Data Type

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

#### Purpose

This property is a container for storing data associated with the type definition.

#### Remarks

Use container subproperties under the
 TypeAttributes
 property to serve as attribute namespaces. National Instruments recommends that you create a uniquely named container or hierarchy of containers under which you store attribute variables, such as
 CompanyName.AttributeCategory.Attribute
 , to avoid name conflicts.

The name
 NI
 is reserved at the root level for National Instruments.

National Instruments recommends that you access this property only if the
 [PropertyObject.HasTypeAttributes](propertyobject-hastypeattributes.html)
 property is
 True
 .

If the object is not a type definition, the property reports an error.

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.Attributes](propertyobject-attributes.html)

[PropertyObject.HasAttributes](propertyobject-hasattributes.html)

[PropertyObject.HasTypeAttributes](propertyobject-hastypeattributes.html)

[PropertyObject.TypeAttributes](propertyobject-typeattributes.html)

### PropertyObject.TypeMinimumTestStandVersion

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).TypeMinimumTestStandVersion

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies the earliest version of TestStand that can use a type.

#### Remarks

When you load a file that contains the type in a version of TestStand that is older than the value of this property, TestStand uses the currently loaded version of the type, if one exists. Otherwise, the file fails to load.

## TOPIC 02138: PropertyObject.TypeVersion

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-typeversion.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-typeversion.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.TypeVersion Data Type String Purpose Specifies the version of the PropertyObject object if it is a root type definition. Remarks If the object is not a root type definition, the property reports an error. Call the PropertyObject.IsRootTypeDefinition property to check if this pr

### PropertyObject.TypeVersion

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).TypeVersion

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies the version of the PropertyObject object if it is a root type definition.

#### Remarks

If the object is not a root type definition, the property reports an error. Call the
 [PropertyObject.IsRootTypeDefinition](propertyobject-isroottypedefinition.html)
 property to check if this property would return an error. The version string is in a format similar to that of DLLs and executables:
 "M[.m[.r[.b]]],"
 where
 M
 =major version,
 m
 =minor version,
 r
 =revision, and
 b
 =build number. All but the major version can be omitted. Example version strings are "1.0.2.200" and "2.1." If you want to set the type version, you must pass a string that follows this format.

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.IsRootTypeDefinition](propertyobject-isroottypedefinition.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Properties

The password you pass for the passwordString parameter must match the password set for the type definition or this method returns an error, even if the

### PropertyObject.UnlockTypeDefinition

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).UnlockTypeDefinition( passwordString)

#### Purpose

Changes the in-memory state of a password-protected type definition to unlocked. The password you pass for the
 passwordString
 parameter must match the password set for the type definition or this method returns an error, even if the type is already in an unlocked state. This method also returns an error if you call it on a type that is not password-protected.

#### Remarks

You can call this method on any property of the type definition, not just the root object of the type.

Note

password-protecting type definitions

 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobject-unserialize.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02140: PropertyObject.Unserialize

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-unserialize.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-unserialize.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.Unserialize( stream, objectName, RWoptions) Purpose This method is obsolete. Use the PropertyObject.UnserializeEx method instead. Remarks Reads the contents of an object from a stream of string data and stores the contents in the PropertyObject to which the method applies. You

### PropertyObject.Unserialize

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).Unserialize( stream, objectName, RWoptions)

#### Purpose

Note

PropertyObject.UnserializeEx

#### Remarks

Reads the contents of an object from a stream of string data and stores the contents in the PropertyObject to which the method applies.

You cannot unserialize a stream that contains a container type into a property object that is a value type, or vice versa. This method does not return an error, but instead sets the PropertyObject on which this method operates to the default value.

If you attempt to unserialize a stream that contains a value type into a property object of a different value type, TestStand attempts to coerce the value. If the coercion is unsuccessful, TestStand sets the PropertyObject on which this method operates to the default value.

TestStand does not assign the name or flags associated with the top-level PropertyObject in the stream to the PropertyObject on which this method operates.

#### Parameters

stream
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies an existing stream of data that stores the object.

objectName
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the name with which the object is stored in the stream.

RWoptions
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more
 [ReadWriteOptions](readwriteoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple read write options.

#### See Also

[Engine.UnserializeObjects](engine-unserializeobjects.html)

[PropertyObject.Serialize](propertyobject-serialize.html)

[PropertyObject.UnserializeEx](propertyobject-unserializeex.html)

[ReadWriteOptions](readwriteoptions.html)

[Thread Safety of the PropertyObject API and TestStand Variables](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_threadsafetyapi)

Parent topic:

Obsolete PropertyObject Methods

 to specify the default behavior, or pass one or more

## TOPIC 02142: PropertyObject.UpdateEnumerators

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-updateenumerators.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-updateenumerators.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.UpdateEnumerators( newValues) Return Value Boolean True if a new enumerator was added, the numeric value of an existing enumerator was changed, the value of IsStrict is changed, or the value of IsFlags is changed. False otherwise. Purpose Replaces the set of enumerators for an

### PropertyObject.UpdateEnumerators

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).UpdateEnumerators( newValues)

#### Return Value

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

True if a new enumerator was added, the numeric value of an existing enumerator was changed, the value of IsStrict is changed, or the value of IsFlags is changed. False otherwise.

#### Purpose

Replaces the set of enumerators for an enumeration data type.

#### Remarks

Call this method on the root type definition of an enumeration data type to specify the set of enumerators for the type. Calling this method on a PropertyObject that is not the root type definition of an enumeration causes a runtime error. Changing the set of enumerators updates all currently loaded instances of the data type.

#### Parameters

newValues
 As
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[In] An array of containers where each container has the following properties:

UpdateEnumeratorsElementProperty_Name ("EnumeratorName") - Enumerator Name (string)

UpdateEnumeratorsElementProperty_EnumeratorValue ("EnumeratorValue") - Enumerator Value (number)

UpdateEnumeratorsElementProperty_OldName ("OldEnumeratorName") [optional] - Prior Name, if renaming (string)

You can specify a new value for the data type's
 IsStrict
 setting by attaching a Boolean attribute to the array with a property path of
 "TestStand.Enum.IsStrict"
 .

You can specify a new value for the data type's
 IsFlags
 setting by attaching a Boolean attribute to the array with a property path of
 "TestStand.Enum.IsFlags"
 .

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.EnumIsValid](propertyobject-enumisvalid.html)

[PropertyObject.Enumerators](propertyobject-enumerators.html)

allowDuplicates
 As
 [Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] PropertyObjects can have identical names when they are elements in an array of PropertyObjects. If the object is not an array element, pass
 False
 to this parameter.

isValid
 As
 [Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[Out] Returns
 True
 if the new name is valid.

## TOPIC 02146: PropertyObject.Write

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject-write.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject-write.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObject.Write( pathString, objectName, RWoptions) Purpose Writes the contents of an object to the file the pathString parameter specifies and associates the name the objectName parameter specifies with the object in the file. Remarks If you call this method on an alias object , TestSta

### PropertyObject.Write

#### Syntax

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html).Write( pathString, objectName, RWoptions)

#### Purpose

Writes the contents of an object to the file the
 pathString
 parameter specifies and associates the name the
 objectName
 parameter specifies with the object in the file.

#### Remarks

If you call this method on an
 [alias object](propertyobject-isaliasobject.html)
 , TestStand generates the stream using the object to which the alias refers. This method does not include alias subproperty objects in the stream.

Note

PropertyObjects

PropertyObject

PropertyObject

PropertyObject

PropertyObject

Lock

PropertyObject

#### Parameters

pathString
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the pathname of the file to which to write the object data.

objectName
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the name to associate with the object.

RWoptions
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass
 0
 to specify the default behavior or pass one or more
 [ReadWriteOptions](readwriteoptions.html)
 constants. Use the bitwise-OR operator to specify multiple read/write options.

If you have already written an object with the specified name to the file, pass the
 RWOption_EraseExistingObject
 constant for this parameter. Otherwise, the values stored in the file do not update to the values of the object you are writing if the object you are writing has default values for some of its properties. Additionally, unless you use the
 RWOption_EraseExistingObject
 or
 RWOption_EraseAll
 constants, the method leaves properties from previously written versions of the object in the file even if the properties do not exist in the current version of the object being written.

#### See Also

[PropertyObject.GetXML](propertyobject-getxml.html)

[PropertyObject.IsAliasObject](propertyobject-isaliasobject.html)

[PropertyObject.ReadEx](propertyobject-readex.html)

[PropertyObject.Serialize](propertyobject-serialize.html)

[ReadWriteOptions](readwriteoptions.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 02147: PropertyObject

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobject.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobject.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the PropertyObject class to manipulate and access the values of variables and custom step properties. You can also use the PropertyObject to add, copy, or delete subproperties of variables and custom step properties. You can create new objects of this class using the Engine.NewPropertyObject met

### PropertyObject

Use the PropertyObject class to manipulate and access the values of variables and custom step properties. You can also use the PropertyObject to add, copy, or delete subproperties of variables and custom step properties.

You can create new objects of this class using the
 [Engine.NewPropertyObject](engine-newpropertyobject.html)
 method. You can obtain existing objects of this class as return values from numerous functions. You can obtain the underlying PropertyObject for objects of every class except the
 Engine
 class by using the
 AsPropertyObject
 method of the respective class.

## TOPIC 02148: PropertyObjectElements

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectelements.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectelements.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use this enumeration to refer to specific parts of a PropertyObject with methods and properties such as Location.Element and SequenceContext.GetMultipleValues . PropertyObjectElement_Attributes –(Value: 7) Specifies the attributes of the PropertyObject , which you access through the PropertyObject.A

### PropertyObjectElements

Use this enumeration to refer to specific parts of a
 [PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)
 with methods and properties such as
 [Location.Element](location-element.html)
 and
 [SequenceContext.GetMultipleValues](sequencecontext-getmultiplevalues.html)
 .

- PropertyObjectElement_Attributes 
 –(Value: 7) Specifies the attributes of the
 PropertyObject 
 , which you access through the
 PropertyObject.Attributes 
 property.
- PropertyObjectElement_Comment 
 –(Value: 3) Specifies the comment of a PropertyObject, which you access through the
 PropertyObject.Comment 
 property.
- PropertyObjectElement_Flags 
 –(Value: 4) Specifies the flags of a PropertyObject, which you access through the
 PropertyObject.GetFlags 
 and
 PropertyObject.SetFlags 
 methods.
- PropertyObjectElement_Name 
 –(Value: 2) Specifies the name of a PropertyObject, which you access through the
 PropertyObject.Name 
 property.
- PropertyObjectElement_None 
 –(Value: 0) Does not specify any part of a PropertyObject.
- PropertyObjectElement_NumericFormat 
 –(Value: 5) Specifies the numeric format of a PropertyObject, which you access through the
 PropertyObject.NumericFormat 
 property.
- PropertyObjectElement_Representation 
 –(Value: 6) Specifies the representation of PropertyObject, which you access with the
 PropertyObjectType.Representation 
 property.
- PropertyObjectElement_Value 
 –(Value: 1) Specifies the value of a PropertyObject, which you access with GetVal and SetVal methods.

#### See Also

[Location.Element](location-element.html)

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[PropertyObject.Comment](propertyobject-comment.html)

[PropertyObject.GetFlags](propertyobject-getflags.html)

[PropertyObject.GetValBinary](propertyobject-getvalbinary.html)

[PropertyObject.NumericFormat](propertyobject-numericformat.html)

[PropertyObject.SetFlags](propertyobject-setflags.html)

## TOPIC 02151: PropertyObjectFile.CheckForModifiedTypes

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-checkformodifiedtypes.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-checkformodifiedtypes.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.CheckForModifiedTypes( dlgTitle, okButtonText, options, versionIncOption, operationCanceled, foundModifiedTypes) Purpose Determines if the PropTypeFlags_IsModifiedType flag is set for any types used within the file. Remarks If a modified type is found, the options parameter

### PropertyObjectFile.CheckForModifiedTypes

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).CheckForModifiedTypes( dlgTitle, okButtonText, options, versionIncOption, operationCanceled, foundModifiedTypes)

#### Purpose

Determines if the
 PropTypeFlags_IsModifiedType
 flag is set for any types used within the file.

#### Remarks

If a modified type is found, the
 options
 parameter determines the specific action to take. If you pass
 CheckForModifiedTypes_Prompt
 to the
 options
 parameter, this method launches a warning dialog box in which you can specify the action, if any, that TestStand takes. The sequence editor calls this method before calling the
 [PropertyObjectFile.WriteFile](propertyobjectfile-writefile.html)
 method to save a sequence file.

#### Parameters

dlgTitle
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies the title of the dialog box. Pass an empty string to use the default title for the dialog box.

okButtonText
 As
 [String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Pass a string to display text on the OK button or pass an empty string to use the default text.

options
 As
 [Long](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] Specifies whether the method launches a warning dialog box if a modified type is found, or whether the method performs a specific action if a modified type is found. Pass one of
 [CheckForModifiedTypesOptions](checkformodifiedtypesoptions.html)
 constants to this method.

versionIncOption
 As
 [TypeVersionAutoIncrement](typeversionautoincrement.html)

[In] Specifies which version number to increment when you pass
 CheckForModifiedTypes_AutoIncrementVersions
 to the
 options
 parameter.

operationCanceled
 As
 [Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[Out] Returns
 True
 if a user clicks
 Cancel
 .

foundModifiedTypes
 As
 [Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[Out] Returns
 True
 if modified types were found in the file.

#### See Also

[CheckForModifiedTypesOptions](checkformodifiedtypesoptions.html)

[PropertyObject.GetTypeFlags](propertyobject-gettypeflags.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.WriteFile](propertyobjectfile-writefile.html)

[PropertyObjTypeFlags](propertyobjtypeflags.html)

[TypeVersionAutoIncrement](typeversionautoincrement.html)

Parent topic:

### PropertyObjectFile.ContentType

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).ContentType

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies the type of file content.

#### Remarks

This property is set by the TestStand engine when creating and reading property object files. You should not change this property for predefined types of property object files, such as sequence files, workspace files, project files, type palette files, and the user file and globals file.

## TOPIC 02158: PropertyObjectFile.FileType

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-filetype.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-filetype.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.FileType Data Type PropertyObjectFileTypes Use the following constants with this data type: FileType_AdaptersConfigFile –(Value: 11) An adapters configuration file. FileType_ConfigFile –(Value: 0) The Engine.ConfigFile file. FileType_CustomConfigFile –(Value: 13) A custom c

### PropertyObjectFile.FileType

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).FileType

#### Data Type

[PropertyObjectFileTypes](propertyobjectfiletypes.html)

Use the following constants with this data type:

- FileType_AdaptersConfigFile 
 –(Value: 11) An adapters configuration file.
- FileType_ConfigFile 
 –(Value: 0) The
 Engine.ConfigFile 
 file.
- FileType_CustomConfigFile 
 –(Value: 13) A custom configuration file.
- FileType_GeneralEngineConfigFile 
 –(Value: 9) A general engine configuration file.
- FileType_ProjectFile 
 –(Value: 6) A TestStand project file.
- FileType_PropertyObjectFile 
 –(Value: 7) A generic PropertyObjectFile.
- FileType_SearchDirectoriesConfigFile 
 –(Value: 10) A search directories configuration file.
- FileType_SequenceFile 
 –(Value: 1) A sequence file.
- FileType_StationGlobalsFile 
 –(Value: 3) The
 Engine.GlobalsFile 
 file.
- FileType_TemplatesFile 
 –(Value: 8) The
 Engine.GetTemplatesFile 
 file.
- FileType_TypePaletteFile 
 –(Value: 2) A type palette file.
- FileType_TypePalettesConfigFile 
 –(Value: 12) A type palettes configuration file.
- FileType_UsersFile 
 –(Value: 4) The
 Engine.UsersFile 
 file.
- FileType_WorkspaceFile 
 –(Value: 5) A
 WorkspaceFile 
 file.

#### Purpose

Returns the type of file.

#### See Also

[PropertyObjectFile.FileTypeDescription](propertyobjectfile-filetypedescription.html)

Parent topic:

Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-filewritingformat.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02160: PropertyObjectFile.FileWritingFormat

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-filewritingformat.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-filewritingformat.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.FileWritingFormat Data Type FileWritingFormats Use the following constants with this data type: FileWritingFormat_Binary –(Value: 2) Specifies that TestStand writes the file in a binary format. This format is the fastest and most memory-efficient format. FileWritingFormat_I

### PropertyObjectFile.FileWritingFormat

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).FileWritingFormat

#### Data Type

[FileWritingFormats](filewritingformats.html)

Use the following constants with this data type:

- FileWritingFormat_Binary 
 –(Value: 2) Specifies that TestStand writes the file in a binary format. This format is the fastest and most memory-efficient format.
- FileWritingFormat_Ini 
 –(Value: 1) Specifies that TestStand writes the file in an INI format. This format is used by previous versions of TestStand (3.
 x 
 or earlier). Use this format when necessary to support existing code that reads the INI file directly.
 Note 
 The INI format is deprecated in TestStand 2019 and may not be supported in future releases.
- FileWritingFormat_Xml 
 –(Value: 3) Specifies that TestStand writes the file in an XML format. Use this format if you want to read, parse, or create files as XML. This option is the most readable and parseable format.

#### Purpose

Specifies the format in which TestStand writes the file.

#### Remarks

Attempting to set to INI (or any other unsupported value) will throw an exception.

#### See Also

[StationOptions.DefaultFileWritingFormat](stationoptions-defaultfilewritingformat.html)

Parent topic:

Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-handletypeconflicts.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02161: PropertyObjectFile.HandleTypeConflicts

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-handletypeconflicts.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-handletypeconflicts.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.HandleTypeConflicts( handlerType) Return Value Boolean Returns True if types were resolved successfully. Purpose Detects and resolves type conflicts that occur after loading a file. Remarks Typically, the PropertyObjectFile.ReadFile method handles type conflicts. The engine

### PropertyObjectFile.HandleTypeConflicts

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).HandleTypeConflicts( handlerType)

#### Return Value

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

Returns
 True
 if types were resolved successfully.

#### Purpose

Detects and resolves type conflicts that occur after loading a file.

#### Remarks

Typically, the
 [PropertyObjectFile.ReadFile](propertyobjectfile-readfile.html)
 method handles type conflicts.

The engine loads the
 [Engine.UsersFile](engine-usersfile.html)
 ,
 [Engine.GlobalsFile](engine-globalsfile.html)
 and
 [Engine.ConfigFile](engine-configfile.html)
 at startup, but does not resolve type conflicts in those files. Therefore, the sequence editor uses this method to resolve type conflicts in those files after it creates the
 [Engine](engine.html)
 object.

#### Parameters

handlerType
 As
 [TypeConflictHandlerTypes](typeconflicthandlertypes.html)

[In] Specifies how type conflicts are handled.

#### See Also

[Engine](engine.html)

[Engine.ConfigFile](engine-configfile.html)

[Engine.GlobalsFile](engine-globalsfile.html)

[Engine.UsersFile](engine-usersfile.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.ReadFile](propertyobjectfile-readfile.html)

[TypeConflictHandlerTypes](typeconflicthandlertypes.html)

Parent topic:

Methods

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.IsModified Data Type Boolean Purpose Returns a value that indicates whether the file has been modified since it was last written to disk. Remarks This property returns True if the change count has increased since the last time the file was written to disk. After reading a f

### PropertyObjectFile.IsModified

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).IsModified

#### Data Type

[Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Returns a value that indicates whether the file has been modified since it was last written to disk.

#### Remarks

This property returns
 True
 if the change count has increased since the last time the file was written to disk.

After reading a file, TestStand might perform automatic type conversions and modify the file. For these files, this property returns
 True
 after the file is read from disk. The
 [PropertyObjectFile.IsModifiedByUser](propertyobjectfile-ismodifiedbyuser.html)
 property only returns
 True
 if the file is modified and TestStand did not perform all the modifications.

[PropertyObjectFile.ChangeCount](propertyobjectfile-changecount.html)

## TOPIC 02169: PropertyObjectFile.Lock

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-lock.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-lock.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.Lock( [passwordString]) Purpose Locks the file. The PropertyObjectFile.Protection property specifies the type of protection for the lock. After reading a protected file, TestStand automatically locks the file. Use the PropertyObjectFile.Unlock method to unlock the file. Rem

### PropertyObjectFile.Lock

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).Lock( [passwordString])

#### Purpose

Locks the file. The
 [PropertyObjectFile.Protection](propertyobjectfile-protection.html)
 property specifies the type of protection for the lock. After reading a protected file, TestStand automatically locks the file. Use the
 [PropertyObjectFile.Unlock](propertyobjectfile-unlock.html)
 method to unlock the file.

#### Remarks

This method applies only to sequence files. Using this method on other files causes an error. Locking a file causes an error when the
 PropertyObjectFile.Protection
 property is set to
 [ProtectedObjectOption_None](protectedobjectoptions.html)
 .

Note

#### Parameters

passwordString
 As
 [Variant](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] [
 [Optional](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_optional_parameters)
 ] Specifies the password for the lock operation. If no
 passwordString
 parameter is specified, the previous password is used. If no previous password was specified, the password is an empty string.

#### See Also

[Omitting Optional Parameters](/csh?context=ts_tsapiref_optional_parameters)

[PropertyObjectFile.Locked](propertyobjectfile-locked.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.Protection](propertyobjectfile-protection.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.Unlock](propertyobjectfile-unlock.html)

[ProtectedObjectOptions](protectedobjectoptions.html)

Parent topic:

Methods

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-requirements.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02175: PropertyObjectFile.Requirements

- bundle_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-requirements.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/teststand-api-reference/raw/resource/enus/tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-requirements.html
- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.Requirements Data Type PropertyObject Purpose Returns the Requirements property for the file. The Links subproperty of the Requirements property is an array of string values that represents the product and unit requirements that the file covers. Remarks This property is val

### PropertyObjectFile.Requirements

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).Requirements

#### Data Type

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

#### Purpose

Returns the Requirements property for the file. The Links subproperty of the Requirements property is an array of string values that represents the product and unit requirements that the file covers.

#### Remarks

This property is valid for sequence files, project files, and workspace files. This property returns an error for all other file types.

You can use the following pseudocode to add a new element to the list of requirements:

PropertyObject links = propertyObjectFile.Requirements.GetPropertyObject("Links", 0);
 int nextAvailableIndex = links.GetNumElements();
 links.SetValStringByOffset(nextAvailableIndex, PropertyOptions.PropOption_InsertElement, "REQ_ABC");

#### See Also

[PropertyObject](propertyobject.html)

[Sequence.Requirements](sequence-requirements.html)

[Step.Requirements](step-requirements.html)

Parent topic:

Properties

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=teststand-api-reference path=tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-savefileifmodified.html language=enus -->

Returns
 False
 only if the user clicked
 Cancel
 in the Prompt dialog box.

#### Purpose

Writes the contents of the file to disk if the file has been modified.

#### Remarks

This method does nothing if the file has not been modified. If the file has been modified, it prompts the user with an option to save, then writes the file. The
 [PropertyObjectFile.Path](propertyobjectfile-path.html)
 property determines the pathname of the file to write.

Note

PropertyObjectFile.WriteFile

#### Parameters

prompt
 As
 [Boolean](data-types-for-teststand.html)

[In] If this parameter is
 True
 and if the file has been modified, a dialog box opens and asks the user whether to save the file.

This parameter has a default value of
 True
 .

#### See Also

[PropertyObjectFile.IsModified](propertyobjectfile-ismodified.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.Path](propertyobjectfile-path.html)

[PropertyObjectFile.WriteFile](propertyobjectfile-writefile.html)

Parent topic:

- source_path: `tsapiref/propertyobjectfile-version.html`

- document_id: `teststand-api-reference`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Syntax PropertyObjectFile.Version Data Type String Purpose Specifies the version string associated with the PropertyObjectFile object. Remarks You can manually set this value to a valid version string where the numbers from left to right denote the Major, Minor, Revision, and Build version. The Test

### PropertyObjectFile.Version

#### Syntax

[PropertyObjectFile](propertyobjectfile.html).Version

#### Data Type

[String](data-types-for-teststand.html)

#### Purpose

Specifies the version string associated with the PropertyObjectFile object.

#### Remarks

You can manually set this value to a valid version string where the numbers from left to right denote the Major, Minor, Revision, and Build version. The TestStand Engine increments the version number each time you save a modified sequence file if you enable the Auto Increment Sequence File Version option on the File tab of the Station Options dialog box. For files that are not sequence files, this property is not used.

### PropertyObjectFile
